<Author>britmom
<Content>Enjoyed the Royal Magda We stayed at the Royal Magda for 2 nights. It was a great location, within 2 minutes walk of the L'Arc du Triomphe and the Metro. Being so close to the top of the Champs Elysee I had expected traffic noise - but the hotel is located down a side street and the area was very quiet. We are a family with 2 young children so we booked the family suite - one king bed and a pullout sofa bed. This worked well for us - our children are 7 and 10 - but may be limiting for older children. The staff, in particular Sebastian and Flore, were extremely helpful and the hotel and our room was very clean. There are plenty of places to eat around this area at reasonable prices. The only downside to this hotel is parking-the street parking is very tight. If you are flying into Paris avoid driving at all costs and use the excellent Metro system - it makes life much easier. As it was our first time in Paris and time was limited we hired a guide for the day, Michael Osman, (---) and he was excellent. Very knowledgable, great with the kids and took us everywhere we wanted to go and more.

<Author>Red123London
<Content>Good location The Royal Magda Etoile is situated very close to the Arc de Triomphe and Champs Elysees and it is within walking distance of most of the major attractions. The nearest metro station was the Charles de Gaulle Etoile, which made it easy to get to anywhere that wasn't within easy walking distance.It's true that the lift is small and our room was also on the small side but as we didn't spend a lot of time there this was not a problem. The walls were thin but we weren't particularly bothered by noise from our neighbors or from the street outside, which was reasonably quiet. The room was clean, the bed was comfortable and the shower was powerful. We didn't make use of the breakfast facilities but it was available until 12:00.I would recommend the Royal Magda for anyone visiting Paris and would stay there again.

<Content>Birthday trip from heaven I took my boyfriend to Paris as a birthday surprise mid march 2007 and booked the Magda due to the great reviews I'd seen on here. WhenI called I mentioned that it was a special occasion and was overjoyedwhen we checked in to find we had been upgraded free of charge to thebest suite in the hotel.Our time in Paris would have not been half as amazing had it not beenfor the marvellous service we received in the hotel. Johan was beyondhelpful and got us a table in a wonderful restaurant overlooking the Seineand Eiffel Tower, when we stepped out of the taxi Johan had called for us we were beneath the Eiffel Tower that was sparkling with lights and lasers, it truly took our breath away and we would never have known to go here or been able to get a table ourselves. Johan offered to get tickets for a show but we didn't have long in Paris and they were quite expensive so we decided to leave it for another time.The room was clean, spacious and comfortable. This isn't a super trendy stylish hotel but it's was perfect for our intimate weekend away. Breakfast was lovely,not a bacon and eggs type affair but most importantly for me good quality coffee served in nice pots and a selection of cheeses, pastries, cereal and dried fruit/yogurt. We only ate breakfast in the hotel but when we came home from our meal we had cocktails in the bar with snacks and talked to the lovely night concierge who made our drinks and was really friendly and interesting. Much to our embarassment and inspite of the fact I studied French til A-Level and was once quite good at it we were beyond appauling when it came to speaking French, thankfully we were put to shame by the impeccable English spoken by Johan and his colleague on the night shift and pretty much every person we came into contact with. Nobody lived up to the snooty Parisian stereotype we were so hoping not to encounter on our first venture over the Channel.The hotel is a 2 minute walk from the Arc de Triomphe and we found the location to be ideal for getting to pretty much everywhere by foot, we only needed transport to and from the airport and for me in my stilettos on our big night out, other than that we walked everywhere.Our return flight was not until late in the evening and we were able to leave our luggage safe all day whilst we saw more of Paris which was a weight off our minds and shoulders.We both agreed that the service we received was without a doubt the best, and most personalised service we have ever received in a hotel.Without Johan's advice and help we could have ended up having a very different experience so we really do owe the success of our trip to him as he made my partner's birthday such a memorable one in many ways. Highly recommended!!!

<Author>chris65NewYorker
<Content>Happy we booked the Royal Magda My family of six, including three children and one senior, stayed at this great little hotel in late March through early April. It was a wonderful value for the money. We have only good things to say...the staff was patient and friendly (despite my rambunctious kids), the rooms were immaculate, and the location was fantastic. The Air France bus from the airport drops you off just two blocks away. The Metro is also two short blocks away, and the Arc/Champs De Elysee is right there. And if you're on a budget, try the restaurant right on the corner...have forgotten the name already, but it was a cafeteria-style restaurant with a price of 9.6 euro for a hot entree, drink, and dessert. You'll pass it on your way to and from the metro.The food is fine and the atmosphere is perfect if you're with kids, as it's a casual place with a relatively high tolerance for noise. Yes, the rooms (and elevator) are small compared to American standards, but aren't they all in Paris? Thank you, Yohan! The Vercelletto Family

<Author>Chester100
<Content>Great location and staff We stayed at the Hotel Magda for 6 nights in late March early April 07. The location is excellent, being only a few minutes walk from the metro station (from which you can easily explore all of Paris' attractions), the Champs Elysees, the Arch de Triumph and plently of cafes and restaurants. The staff are very helpful, accomodating and courteous and they all speak English very well (which was great because my French is terrible). We stayed in a club room on the fourth floor, which consisted of 2 single beds. The room is very small (which is standard for Europe) but very clean, comfortable and quite adequate considering the very reasonable price. The room had a view of the street below and apartments opposite, and considering the central location of the hotel there was not a lot of noise. My partner did notice noise coming through the wall of neighbouring rooms, but this was minor.We had breakfast at the hotel, which consisted of coffee or tea (bottomless cup), cereals, fruit, cold cuts and an assortment of pastries. The breakfast costs extra, and although it seemed a bit expensive it was convenient and plentiful. However, we did notice quite a few cafes serving breakfast nearby, which looked like they would be viable options. I would happily stay at this hotel again.

<Author>MicaBelfast
<Content>value for money I stayed at this hotel for 3 nights in March 07' with my husband and young children and would recommend it for most travellers.The hotel undoubtedely has a fantastic location - literally turn the street corner and your faced with the Arc de Triomphe. The hotel is small, well run and clean with staff who are very helpful and pleasant. We booked a Junior Suite which was spacious with a large double bed and a very comfortable sofa bed. Unfortunately the rooms look out onto a small court yard but considering the price and the location, its not a big deal. The only other details that may need to be taken into consideration is that the lift is tiny and therefore more than one trip may be required for luggage/ prams etc. and the walls are a little on the thin side but these are very insignificant gripes when taking into account all the many positives the hotel has to offer.

<Content>Very pleasant and comfortable stay - first time in paris Booked through venere.com at an excellent rate, we arrived sans baggage thanks to US Airways misconnects but our disappointment with our luggage quickly eroded when we checked in. The staff are extremely helpful and pleasant, with excellent english, and the hotel itself is cute, efficient in use of space and felt very comfortable. Nice comfortable yet firm mattress in our room and open windows that were tall balcony like so plenty of air. Quiet side street but main roads a few blocks away so some noise, but we are in a city.....Bathrooms and showers were very nice (good hot shower) and whilst the room was small, this is what you would expect for a decent inner city hotel. Fantastic location (Arc de Triomph), near RER/Metro lines, and right next to the Air France bus so getting to and from airport is trivially simple, timely and cheap. Theres a bar up the block and across the street open to 2am (La Flamme) expensive but nice for a late night night cap, though cocktails there were a bit low on the kick side :)We didnt try the breakfast or bar in the hotel - there are plenty of places in the city. Would I stay again ? Absolutely. Any newbies to Paris - hit the Marais area, latin Quarter, St Germain area, and spend time on foot as well as on metro for a quick intro to great city.-Mark  Heather

<Author>gofar
<Content>Great Staff and location At first we thought the location was a little off the beaten track,but once we discovered the Metro and how simple it was to use,we quickly changed our minds.It is is a commercial district with limited number of restaurants but very close to a Metro Station and all the shops .Museums and attractions are minutes away by Metro.The hotel itself is very clean and the staff are very friendly and helpful.We stayed in the larger Club Rooms as past experience of Parisian Hotels tell us that rooms in general tend to be very functional and small.The Club rooms were normal sized rooms with good room service,flat screen tv,mini bar etc.Close by we were referred to the Chez Clement Restaurant for a nice dinner and it was excellent.For a little fun try the Happy Hours in the various Latin Quarter pubs,located by Metro to St Michael District. Taxi service in Paris is poor so dont miss the last Metro at 12.30am.We skipped breakfast,as 鈧?2 per head was a little steep,and the breakfast area lacked atmosphere (looked like a train carriage).Plenty of nice breakfast eateries nearby.

<Author>Vikingstad
<Content>Royal Magda Etoile reviews are true! What a lovely hotel, especially for 99 Euros a night in mid-January. The hotel is a mere block from the Arc de Triomphe and two blocks from the Air France Express Bus to CDG Airport. The service was friendly, and everyone spoke English when my French stumbled.I traveled solo for a long week-end holiday to the City of Lights. Although my room was small, it was certainly more than adequate enough for me. The sheets were soft and comfortable, the room and bathroom were immaculately serviced each day, and there was wireless internet access available. For such a small hotel, I was surprised to find that the hotel offers room service and a mini-bar (although I did not partake in either).The breakfast may be expensive for some at 12 Euros (it was not included in the room price I was quoted), but it consisted of a nice assortment of breads, croissants, cereals, yogurt, meats and cheeses. The breakfast area is quiet and comfortable--a nice place to plan your day over an endless cup of hot coffee.Overall, I find it hard to believe you can beat the value this hotel offers.HINT: Although most people would rather visit Paris during the spring and summer when Paris is in full bloom, don't neglect this city during the off months. Airfares are a bargain (I paid $550 round-trip from Newark Liberty), the tourist sites are empty, and in January especially, all of the stores have great sales. Even with the weaker dollar, I spent over $300 on great deals at the Men's store Madelios.

<Content>Great Hotel. What more can I say? It was time for another visit to Paris. This time however, it would be to take my grand mother along. This hotel was chosen because of the size of the rooms and the fabulous reviews it receives from Tripadvisor members.The hotel did not disappoint. As promised the hotel was in a quiet part of town, and it was close to virtually everything. The Arc De Triomphe was only a 5 minute walk away as well as the Charles de Gaulle metro station. The junior suite we where in was pretty large and is probably comfortable for 2 couples or a couple and 2 children. The Hotel room consisted of a large bedroom with a queen size bed, and LCD screen, the living room had a sofa that converted into a twin size bed. The living room had a mini bar as well as a regular TV. The bathrooms where very big too, and was pretty modern. The rooms where cleaned everyday and the complimentary toiletries where refilled each day.The front desk was very helpful, and spoke excellent English. The staff at this hotel where excellent, they made our stay very pleasant. The following are things that we where a bit disappointed at. First of the doors to each room should be upgraded, because they are so thin, you could virtually hear everybody in the hallway, especially at night when guests come back. The hotel elevator fits 2 people only! But hey it鈥檚 better than having no elevator at all, but still it would be nice if they had a little bigger elevator.Parking in Paris is expensive, so if you鈥檙e going to stay at this hotel and you have a car there is an underground parking garage 3 blocks down (Expensive). Unless of course, if your lucky enough to find street parking right in front of the hotel (Ask how long you can park there).We enjoyed our stay very much, and would definitely recommend this hotel to anybody. We would definitely return to this hotel if or when we come back to Paris.

<Author>MacDeeIreland
<Content>Great Hotel. Couldn't fault the professionalism or the location. We booked this Hotel based on the Tripadvisor recommendation (I wanted to test how good and accurate the reviews were). We stayed Dec 1st -4th. Having stayed in the Georges V and the Hotel Napoleon nearby previously, I have to agree with the positive reviews of the hotel. The management and staff were extremely professional and helpful. When our flight was cancelled in Charles De Gaulle, Air France put us up in a Hotel near the Airport Campus, however once we arrived there, I phoned the Hotel Royal Magda and we were able to check back in for another night. Superb.The rooms are very clean and pleasant. The restaurant serves breakfast but, to be honest with so many fantastic restaurants within walking distance, we never used it.I would recommend this Hotel to anyone who doesn't enjoy large touristy hotels with impersonal service.We will be back in February. <Author>Drzava
<Content>Excellent Booked this hotel on the strength of Tripadvisor reviews - as usual they were spot on! We arrived on Jan 1st to find (a) we had been upgraded to a club room as it was our first time in Paris and (b) a Happy New Year card and box of chocolates in our room. Good start! The room itself was reasonably sized (it was one of the larger rooms) with a decent bathroom. Desk, table and a few chairs, along with aircon. Bathroom had a shower in a bathtub. Minibar prices reasonable compared to those in bars and restaurants (shocking!). I am docking one star though because there was intermittent machinery noise (lift or boiler?) throughout the night at the back of the hotel. This was not especially loud but, as I a light sleeper, I had to buy earplugs after the first night. There were no other disturbances. All staff we dealt with were friendly, tolerated my pidgin French, and spoke good English.Location is excellent. It seems to be a little bit out from the centre but the large Metro/RER station at the Arc de Triomphe (round the corner) ensures rapid access to any part of Paris you wish. There are also dozens of restaurants and bars in the immediate area of the hotel, so eating in the evening is absolutely no problem.

<Author>granipc
<Content>Absolutely Wonderful!!! Our first trip to Paris, and the tone was set perfectly by this delightful little hotel! We stayed from the day after Christmas until New Year's Eve and enjoyed every minute. We just really cannot say enough about their incredibly gracious staff, especially Kais and the darling little blond girl at the front desk. Everyone, down to the cleaning staff, were incredibly friendly and helpful and I certainly hope the management recognizes what gems they have in their staff!We arrived well before check-in time, but our rooms were available and ready to be occupied, this was such a treat considering the long overnight flight we had just arrived from.The location is outstanding, so convenient to the Metro, restaurants, shopping, the Arc... it goes on and on! We found the continental breakfast to be the perfect start to our day, and although many commented on the price, we found it worth the convenience. It's also nice they serve breakfast until noon. The staff in the dining room were wonderful.We also enjoyed late night drinks in the comfortable chairs in the lobby (Merci, Kais!) after we returned from dinner on several evenings.The rooms were spotless, and the cleaning staff did a fabulous job, even straightening up our luggage and kid's various odds and ends they had left around the room. We had a suite, which was more than spacious (and we are Americans who are used to LARGE rooms) for our family of four (kids ages 7 and 12), my mother and brother and his wife each had standard double rooms. Only smaill inconvenience was the occasional disco music from the restaurant next door on a couple of evenings that disturbed my mother and brother, who had rooms adjacent to their walls. Nothing too terrible, and didn't go on too late into the night.They also arranged a car to take us back to the airport, and he was terrific! When he couldn't pull right up to the curb because of so much traffic, he parked in the garage, took all our luggage in for us (7 bags, plus some!) and made sure he got us directly to the correct check-in area. All in all, a terrific experience and we will recommend you to all!!! Thank you so much for helping to make this such a wonderful memory for our family!The Mallinger FamilyHouston, Texas

<Author>MagsAndDan
<Content>Christmas in Paris We spent a magical Christmas Eve and Christmas day in this lovely hotel.The excellent service began before our arrival,with Yohan confirming our booking and also helping out with information about getting there, local attractions and eating out.The hotel was easy to get to as it is very near to the impressive Arc De Triomphe. Yohan suggested taking the AirFrance bus from CDG airport instead of the Metro as it avoids having to change stations whilst carting luggage around. We took his advice both ways!The front of the hotel is probably the best looking out of all the buildings on this side street and the reception area of the hotel is very pleasant.The double room we booked was suprisingly large, very quiet and clean. The bathroom was a bit on the small side but again, it was very clean with modern decor. The toilet was separate and again rather small but adequate.The only staff we encountered were Yohan and the gentleman on reception in the evening (we never got his name!). Both spoke excellent english and were very helpful. On the first evening we were directed to a great brasserie a couple of streets away on Ave. De La Grande Armee (the SCS La Grande Armee). Although it may seem a bit pricey to some at 100 euros for two people, the meals were great. As a side note, if you plan to go to this brasserie, brush up on your french food as we had a bit of difficulty with the menu!On the subject of food, the hotel does do meals as there is a menu in the room, although we never did get to try it. We found breakfasts to be adequate for self service Continental style fayre.There was a nice touch on Christmas Day when we arrived back at the hotel to find a Christmas card and chocolates from the staff. Also, Yohan was very helpful in keeping our luggage for a few hours after we checked out as we had some time to kill whilst waiting for our flight. Overall, our experience of this hotel has been one of a pleasant surprise. We didn't quite know what to expect with various tales of small rooms being the norm in Paris. We actually downgraded from a four star hotel to this three star hotel after finding all the positive reviews from TripAdvisor. One of the key benefits is the location, being very close to the Arc de Triomphe, the Champs de Elysees (for big name shops such as Louis Vuitton, Cartier, and DG) and a metro station only 5 minutes away. We will definitely come here again!Dan  Magda

<Author>kurokuroneko
<Content>Great staff and nice location! - Friendly, and very helpful staff. Always a smile!- Housecleaning staff very good. Everything was spotless.- It is very close to the Arc de Triumphe and the Metro/RER. Very nice location.- The buffet breakfast is 12E. A basic selection, but items are fresh.- The room was nicely sized and clean. Our room overlooked the street. Noise was not a problem except for the trash truck in the morning one time during the week. There is a theatre across the street, but the noise was not excessive. Actually, you may find a little more noise from your neighbors as the walls seem to be a little thin. - The shower was prone to leaking on the floor if you angled the spout a bit high. The soap is rather small so we ended up buying some at L'Occitane nearby. Bathroom lacks a facecloth.- There are 2 supermarkets nearby. A small one just around the corner at the end of the street and a bit more upscale one (Monoprix) at the next square. - No alarm clock in the room.- Safebox in the room.- Yes, the elevator is small and new. Just enough for two people.- We used a shared shuttle van to the airport (42E for two people). Professional and door to door service. Airport Connection is the name of the company.- Reasonable selection of restaurants nearby. There are 2 safety items that i was a little concerned about.- Lack of fire detector in the room. All other areas seemed to have detectors and fire safety equipment.- The door does not lock automatically upon entry or exit. In fact, you need to lock yourself in the room. In an emergency, it might be difficult to find your key and then get the door unlocked. You will find there are two doors to the room. The inner one does not lock. Whenever we were in the room, we left our key in the door.Overall, i enjoyed my stay in this hotel and would recommend it without hesitation. Service and location are two key points of this hotel. I would definitely stay there again.

<Author>QP
<Content>Great in everyway, prime location and attentive staff We stayed at Hotel Royal Magda for 4 nights during the Thanksgiving week. I highly recommend this hotel to leisure travelers for the following reasons: - LOCATION: it's 2 blocks away from the Air France les cars (shuttle to/from the airports) stop at the arc de triomphe; half a block away from the CDG Etoile metro station, walking distance to the arc, champs elyssess- Cleaness of room: the hotel was recently renovated, the room/bathroom were extremely clean; elevator's tiny but brand new and functional- Staff: Staff greeted us by name when we checked in; extremely helpful; Johan and Flore were wonderful; they even kept copies of email messages I had sent before my arrivalThings to remember: although almost everything exceeded my expecttations, this is after all a 3 star hotel. It wouldn't be reasonable to expect service anytime with a phone call. Breakfast is usually not included and costs a lot for what you get. Amenities were adequate but limited. Street noise could be a bit of a problem during weekend.TRAVEL TIPS:- Please be sure to purchase the Carte Orange for unlimited metro rides if you're staying longer than a week (calendar week)- The best place visited while in Paris: Pere Lachaise cementary!!!!- Museums: allow plenty of time (at least 3 days) to visit the Louvre, Orsay, Rodin if you like museums- Shopping: makes NO sense to buy anything other than cheeses, chocolate and designer items (Louis Vuitton, Balenciaga). Most items, even French brands, are more expensive in Paris; weak US dollars don't help this matter

<Author>chitownmel
<Content>Can't wait to return! I found out about the Hotel Magda through Trip Advisor back in September. My husband and I just returned from Thanksgiving weekend in Paris. The Hotel Magda did not disappoint. We were immediately upgraded to a suite upon our arrival - at ten am! Allowing us to check into our room so early (after an eight hour flight) was fantastic. The only thing missing was a down comforter, but in Paris, I could do without!The hotel is in an amazing location about two blocks from the Arc de Triomphe. It is also two blocks away from Metro line 1 which is one of the main arteries of the city. It took us almost everywhere we needed to go - and we only had to transfer once to get anywhere else. This was ideal. We never had to take a taxi.We ate breakfast in the hotel each day which was convenient, but there were also many options close by. I would highly recommend the restaurant Citrus Etoile which was only a few blocks away from the hotel. It is operated by an American woman, Elizabeth, and her husband who is a French native. We had our best meal at their restaurant.The staff at the Hotel Magda was extremely helpful and attentive. I am grateful to all of those who reveiwed the hotel before me b/c I probably wouldn't have found this gem otherwise. I can't wait to return!

<Author>MorningMartin
<Content>Excellent in every respect I booked this hotel after reading the excellent reviews on Trip Advisor. I took my fiance and a couple of our friends to Paris for my fiance's birthday and we spent two nights at the hotel. I had emailed the hotel beforehand a couple of times to make some prior enquiries and arrangements and Yohan and Flore were always prompt in replying and giving me the information I needed. Upon arrival, Yohan greeted us at reception and knew who we were instantly, which was a nice personal touch. He also upgraded us at no extra cost to a Junior Suite room which we found to be very nice, clean and spacious. The room was very nicely decorated with lovely decor and the bathroom was a perfect size with lovely clean towels, bathrobe and handy little bottles of shampoo, shower gel and some nice little bath salts. On the evening of my fiance's birthday, Yohan and his Manager (sorry, I cannot recall his name!) recommended to us a lovely Brasserie about 5 mins taxi journey from the airport and went to the trouble of booking the restaurant and taxi for us. Yohan even joined us on his night off at the end of our meal for dessert and helped us sort out a minor problem at the restaurant when they attempted to rip us off by charging us for something we did not order - our French not being particularly good, Yohan was able to rectify this with the waiter!Breakfast was an additional 12 Euros per person but we preferred to venture out to find small cafes for breakfast instead, purely because we wanted to get out of the hotel quickly in the mornings to do our sightseeing. I am told that this hotel has recently been refurbished and you can definitely tell. The decor throughout was very sophisticated and tasteful and I particularly liked the leopard print carpet !Overall we could not fault the hotel in any way, okay maybe the lift is a bit on the small side, but this would not affect anyone wanting to stay there, unless they are just plain fussy! The staff at the hotel were extremely friendly and nothing was too much trouble for them. The location of the hotel is also ideal, the nearest metro being just five minutes walk and right near the Arc de Triomphe and Champs Elysees. The area is extremely quiet and we did not experience any noise from the neighbouring properties.We will definitely be returning to Paris in the Spring/Summer of 2007 for another short break and will without a doubt be booking the Royal Magda for our stay.

<Author>Bussman
<Content>Great hotel I just got back after a 4 day stay in Paris and this hotel indeed deserves it's reputation as being one of the better rated hotels in Paris. Booked the hotel through the reviews from this website and being the first time using it's reviews, was abit nervous but keen on finding out what all the good reviews was all about.The hotel was ideally located at the Arc De Triomphe, only a street away from the bus stop (if taking the Air France bus from CDG airport) and just behind the CDG Etoile metro stop. We arrived early in the morning and the reception staff were kind, polite, receptive and allowed us to store our bags while waiting for our room to be ready (and we actually left and started sightseeing anyways!)We had a club room on one of the higher floors. It was suprisingly very large, spacious and spotless. Having done quite alot of travelling, I was extremely impressed with the cleanliness which was one of the things that I'm particularly fussy about. There was a tiny bit of music noise (still trying to sus out where it came from !) on the first night but the remainder of the nights were quiet. We decided not to have breakfast in the hotel because essentially there were loads of cafes/restaurants in the area. For those who are fastfood addicts, there's a McDonalds  round the corner. We managed to walk to most Paris sights from the hotel easily but the CDG Etoile metro afforded access to most of Paris without much problems. We tended to go for walks at night to witness Paris by night and felt safe walking around the hotel late(though we were back by midnight).To give a fair critique, i've noticed that the mattress was quite firm but I guess that's personal preference. For the claustraphobic ones, the lift is quite cosy.To summarise, my partner is already bugging me to come back to Paris again and we would definitely come back to the Royal Magda.

<Content>Great hotel - easily worth the rating I stayed here for 3 nights with my boyfriend and booked it purely on reviews on this website. I must say the hotel was exceedingly clean and welcoming. <Author>Gab45
<Content>Excellent, but has faults The Hotel Royal Magda Paris is a very quaint hotel in an excellent part of Paris. It is approx 5 min saunter to the Le Arc De Triomphe and the famous Champs Elysees. There are some excellent bars and restaurants in the area and if you are travelling from Ireland through Beauvais it is about 鈧?0 in a taxi to the drop off point. But there is one draw back to the hotel and that is one of the rooms is located next to a very busy restaurant / bar (Room 115) avoid this room or bring sleeping tablets. The breakfast is over priced as you will get similar if not better in a cafe close by. You choose sitting eating a croissant looking at the Le Arc De Triomphe or a dinning room wall for twice the price. All in all I think if I was returning I would consider staying there again taking on board the comments above.

<Author>Davred
<Content>what a location! My first trip to Paris in 40 years! Off I went, accompanied by my 25 year old son who had been in Paris only last year....as a backpacker. His first reaction to the hotel was what a location. There it was, just near the Arc de Triomphe, just around the corner from the Champs d'Elysees, with a metro station only 3 or 4 minutes walk away, and in a narrow street that was relatively quiet.The reception was friendly and quiet and we used the small lift - 1 person plus big bag at a time! - to get to our 4th floor room. With twin beds it was cosy, but we had enough spave. There was an LCD TV on the wall, windows that opened wide, and a bathroom that was modern and well fitted out. The airconditioning was a bit tempremental but adequate for October.We found the room to be quiet, clean, well furnished and comfortable. It was easier to use the stairs to go down to breakfast in the morning. Breakfast was OK without being brilliant, although at 12 euros each, was a tad expensive. We thought we'd breakfast out on Sunday morning, but nothing open nearby - well, except for McDonalds, and so we ended up back at the hotel. A captive audience?I said the room was quiet. On the Friday and Saturday nights there was some late noise from a private club opposite. It was more some noisy patrons leaving late than noise from the club, but it was enough to wake me up. Overall not a big problem though.Advice about getting around Paris was a bit light on at the front desk. The guy who was on duty in the morning knew a lot more than the Night Manager, but everyone was reasonable friendly, didn't laugh at our schoolboy French, and tried to help.I'll certainly return to this hotel and recommend it strongly.

<Author>indiebands
<Content>Very nice hotel, helpful staff We stayed at the Royal Magda for a friend's wedding in October. Overall, we enjoyed our stay there thoroughly and were very happy with the helpfulness of the desk staff. We would stay there again in the future if the prices do not increase (we did have the benefit of a group rate from the wedding).The hotel has recently been refurbished and has genuinely comfortable bathrooms, at least in the suite where we stayed with our 2 year old son. Breakfast in the room at the same price as downstairs was a plus. For a 3 star hotel in the center of Paris, the prices are not bad at all. The location is very convenient to the metro and to the Air France CDG bus. I do wish that we had taken them up on their suggestion of the little brightly red painted french restaurant next door open since 2000 painted tongue in cheek on the outside. The in room safe was vulnerable to reprogramming by our two year old son (what would not be?), but despite being very busy, the hotel staff was able to make an emergency visit to unlock it for us so that we could dress for the wedding. Aparently they were ranked number 1 in Paris hotels on tripadvisor prior to the unfortunate incident where they had to relocate a guest due to the illness of a baby staying at the hotel. The desk staff explained that the incident resulted in an unavoidable inconvenience for the other party who had reserved the room. As a parent, I'd have to say that I side with the hotel on that decision. I recommend this hotel.

<Author>Calistoga Grower
<Content>Believe the reviews, this place is great! Reviews from other travelers make the Hotel Royal Magda sound like the ideal base to explore Paris. Those reviews are highly accurate! We stayed at the Hotel Royal Magda in September and found the rooms to be exceptionally comfortable and spotlessly clean. The staff was friendly, knowledgeable and genuinely warm. We arrived at 9 a.m. after a redeye flight from San Francisco. Check in time is 2 p.m., the norm for most hotels in Paris or anywhere else for that matter. The staff at the Royal Magda seated us in their lobby caf茅 and told us they would immediately clean our room and have it ready within half an hour. By the time we had finished with the coffee and croissants that had appeared in front of us, they had moved our luggage into our room and presented us with a key. The location is perfect, a three-minute walk to a metro station located virtually under the Arc de Triumph. A wide range of restaurants is within a two-block range. On the same block as the hotel are a very good and inexpensive Japanese sushi takeout counter and Guy Savoy where dinner for two with a nice bottle of wine starts around $500. Believe all these glowing reviews. They are accurate.

<Author>tknm
<Content>Very nice hotel in great location! My husband and I spent 6 nights (Sept 7-13) here and for the most part were very happy. I spent many hours searching trip advisor and the internet for a place to stay. I always worry about finding a hotel in another country that will be in a nice area, affordable, and up to my expectations (which my husband says are too high). Given the great reviews on this site I felt comfortable booking at this hotel and was glad to find I had made a good choice.The staff was very friendly and spoke English perfectly, although we did not converse with them much.We were very happy with the room. They look just as the pictures on the website show. Not often do you find the pictures to actually be accurate. The room was cleaned spotless everyday. We had a junior suite that was nice and big. The toilet was in a separate area from the shower/tub which was nice. The decor was very pleasant however there was no room for toiletries in the bathroom so be prepared to use a shelf in the closet.I had originally planned to book a club room but they were not available when I booked. We saw into one of those rooms and it looked like it was nice sized and would have been fine. We also saw into a standard room and that looked very small and cramped. However depending on how much time you spend in the room this hotel can accommodate everyone's taste.It was nice to have the option of air-conditioning as it got quite warm the last few days of our stay but most nights we just slept with a window open slightly and were very comfortable.Free internet access in the rooms was a plus.The location was great and close to the Metro. We did not eat at the hotel so I can't comment on the breakfast however 12 euros seemed quite a lot to pay for breakfast.One issue we did have, although I can't really fault the hotel, was the people in the room above us. They were traveling with what appeared to be twins about 2 years old and had no common sense or courtesy to those guests in the rooms around them. The first 2 nights we listened to them running back and forth across the floor and crying until after 2:00am. and the father repeating over and over stop it. We asked about switching rooms and were told that those people were moving. It turned out they only moved for 2 nights and then were back above us. (The 2 nights they were somewhere else were very quitet ). We did not ask to be moved again as we didn't realize it until the 5th night that they were back and we only had 1 more to go. I admit we did not complain to the front desk as we should have but could not believe those people could be so insensitive and rude to the other guests. I would encourage anyone traveling with small children to consider those others around you that may be enjoying some time away from their own kids and plan your days so as not to disrupt the routines your children are accustomed to causing them to be disruptive at odd hours.Overall I would highly recommend this hotel and would definately consider staying here again if we visit Paris in the future.

<Content>Love the Royal Magda Hotel! Just returned from a month in Paris and Italy and I must say that the Royal Magda was a highlight of my travels! I was with a large group of people that are all different ages and have different preferences and everyone loved the time we spent at this hotel!First, the hotel is in a great location about 1.5 blocks from the Arc di Triomphe and the Champs Elysees. It is easy to walk everywhere, get to a major metro line, and never once felt unsafe (even at 3am). The hotel itself is new and clean with a great sitting area by the bar to hang out and have a glass of wine with friends. There are 5 or 6 floors with a lift that was of typical size for European hotels. We were able to fit 2 people, 2 bags and a wedding dress if it helps! The rooms are the same size as all Paris hotels and wonderfully clean with great and very clean bathrooms. There is a safe and tv on the wall that gets both cnn and bbc news. The rooms have AC so you can have a nice cold room, even if it is hot or muggy in Paris! Even though it is a great hotel at great rates, the best part of the hotel is the concierge, our new friend Yohan. He was the only one working during the day while we were there but I hear Flore is just as great. Yohan planned everything for us from helping wiht hotels, flights, restaurant reservations, what to do and see, directions, tours, ect. And he is just great to talk to and hang out with!

This 3 star hotel is well appointed with a small bar, a comfortable breakfast and lobby sitting area, clean standard rooms, affordable suites, and roomy bathrooms having bathtubs with standing showers and heated towel bars. The Hotel Royal Magda鈥檚 location puts you within 3 to 4 blocks of either the Arc de Triomphe or the Avenue des Champs Elysees and within a 4 to 5 block walk to the Air France bus stop for Charles de Gaulle international airport. But what really sets the Hotel Royal Magda Hotel apart from other 3 star hotels that we have stayed in Paris is the service! While most of our dealings were with Yohan, the daytime manager, our interactions with other staff members were also very pleasant. We were in Paris for the marriage of our youngest daughter. Yohan accomplished all of this extremely efficiently and with good humor. Yohan and the Hotel Royal Magda are both a class act that our family recommends highly!

<Author>Eibhlin2
<Content>Great value in the heart of Paris We have just returned from a two night stay in this excellent hotel in the heart of Paris. With 6 in our party - 2 adults and 4 children - we found it difficult to find reasonably priced accommodation close to the popular visitor attractions. We found a gem in the Royal Madga. A junior suite accommodated 4 of us and a double room directly across the small hall was perfect for the other 2. The junior suite had 2 rooms with a double bed in one and a double bed settee in the other. A large bathroom, flat screen TV and spacious wardrobes made this an ideal room. The double bedroom had a small veranda onto a quiet street. The hotel was spotless, the staff friendly, helpful and courteous. The location was perfect - a stone's throw from the Arc de Triomphe and the Champs Elysees. While tea and coffee making facilities are not provided there was no problem giving us a kettle to make tea - very welcome after a long day exploring this beautiful city. We would highly recommend this hotel to anyone but especially to those travelling with children. We'll be back.  
<Date>Aug 18, 2006

<Author>hlc219
<Content>Wonderful Boutique Hotel This is not an exaggeration! This place is really a must stay. It is two blocks from the Arc de Triomphe and metro. One block away from the Champs Elysee! Location usually means expensive prices or seedy accomodations. The Royal Magda has all the benefits but none of the disadvantages of a ideally located hotel! It was my mother's birthday and I wanted to take my parents to a nice Paris hotel for their first visit to Europe, but I did not want to spend a fortune. I searched everywhere until a found the reviews for the Royal Magda. It looked amazing on the website, so I decided to book. It was also quite affordable. With all of this going for it, I was quite anxious that the hotel would be completely booked, but they had one room left that met our needs!When we arrived (in the wee hours of the morning), all my expectations were exceeded. I found the pictures on the hotel website to be true to life. The staff is wonderful (especially Yohan who helped us through flight cancellations). The hotel accomodated us without interruption for one extra night when our flight was cancelled. The rooms are clean, pretty and modern (flat screen television). The bathrooms are so clean and HUGE! There is also cute little bar and dining area. You can eat breakfast in the hotel but we did not so I can't really say how it was.I will be staying at this hotel the next time and every time I come to Paris until I start making enough money to stay at the Ritz. Even then, I may still choose to stay at the Magda!

<Author>Nicotinia
<Content>Great place We have recently spent a few wonderful days in Paris. This hotel added to the pleasure of the visit. The hotel has a relaxed atmosphere and the staff are very helpful. Our room was very clean and provided a small verandah, a safe, a minibar, flat-screen satelite TV and a hairdryer. The en-suite was fully functional and we were provided with lots of well-laundered towels. OK, we expect all this nowadays, but are sometimes disappointed - but not here. The reception area is compact, as is the lift. The location (a short walk from the Arc de Triomphe) is excellent both for walking to the Champs Elysee and for the Metro. There are many excellent restaurants nearby. If we return to Paris, we plan to stay at this hotel again.
